# Extract relevant data from the table
relevant_cells = []
for row in range(len(table['data'])):
    for col in range(1, len(table['columns'])): # start at column index 1 to skip 'no in series'
        if table['data'][row][col] != "n / a":
            relevant_cells.append({"row_index": row, "column_name": table['columns'][col]})


# Calculate the number of episodes
episode_count = sum([cell["row_index"] for cell in relevant_cells])

# Check if there is more than a dozen episodes
if episode_count > 12:
    answer = "TRUE"
else:
    answer = "FALSE"

Determined column indices: no_in_series={relevant_cells[0]['row_index']} and no_in_season={relevant_cells[1]['row_index']}
Found {episode_count} episodes in the third season.
{answer}
"""
